Def. (function differentiable): f is differentiable at x₀ if ^yVGnXC1S

E and is finite. f is differentiable if this holds for whole
domain of f ^dBf0CdAW

Computation examples ^xcQeYIUc

if f is differentiable in x₀ ⟶ f is continuous at x₀ ^psGnhCFF

continuous non-differentiable functions ^5RT3ZZT2

f(x)=|x| ^PcOPVnFb

## Embedded Files
6886b29d0da7516ef6469077d11264e5d8993b03: $$\lim_{ h \to 0 } \frac{f(x_{0}+h)-f(x_{0})}{h}=f'(x_{0})$$

eade45d421f5350c67fc511d86b21111f7d565ed: $$\displaylines {
f(x)=ax+b   \\ 
\frac{f(x_{0}+h)-f(x_{0})}{h}=\frac{a(x_{0}+h)+b-(ax_{0}+b)}{h} \equiv a \\
}$$

6fbcf454ce3a56b93fd989ede06b3734e550e457: $$\displaylines {
f(x)=x^2   \\ 
\frac{f(x_{0}+h)-f(x_{0})}{h}=\frac{(x_{0}+h)^2-(x_{0})^2}{h} \equiv 2x_{0}+h = 2x_{0} \\
}$$

f1b873cb25cc2c3cf6aef07b840a924ea8f96f98: $$\displaylines {
f(x)=e^x   \\ 
\frac{f(x_{0}+h)-f(x_{0})}{h}=\frac{e^{x_{0}+h}-e^{x_{0}}}{h} = \frac{e^{x_{0}}(e^h-1)}{h} \equiv \frac{e^h-1}{h}e^{x_{0}} = e^{x_{0}} \\
}$$

5150eef7a47e219228d673838f384d73d4701298: $$\displaylines {
f(x_{0}+h)=h\cdot \frac{f(x_{0}+h)-f(x_{0})}{h} + f(x_{0}) \\
\lim_{ h \to 0 }f(x_{0}+h)=0\cdot f'(x_{0})+f(x_{0})=f(x_{0}) \\
\text{set } x=x_{0}+h \qquad \lim_{ x \to x_{0} } f(x)=f(x_{0})
}$$

6c446a59aeb9fc216f284c683c6aa355cdb4a90a: $$(f+g)'=f'+g'$$

0dccbc7e4a93f212e332aa2a8add95b8872d2c4e: $$(fg)'=f'g+fg'$$

cf94d0f5b797176792c5187fee172ef64862cc2a: $$\left( \frac{1}{g} \right)'=-\frac{g'}{g^2}$$

09b4420e3610c40fda1433f09f572f5e5706cbd9: $$\left( \frac{f}{g} \right)'=\frac{f'g-fg'}{g^2}$$

f662327405cc97b19a618a4ec1f437cecc7c225b: $$g'(y)=\frac{1}{f'(x)} \quad y=f(x)$$

2800a5c0c67a572909624308410a40a526b71220: $$h(x)=g(f(x)) ⟶ h'(x)=g'(f(x))\cdot f'(x)$$
